<Name>Jacob Levy<//Name><time>1562652051345<//time><rate>5</rate><Text>Before getting into the review itself, I should say I am very pleased with every aspect of Miracle Ear the company and the product, as well as my experience with the staff at the office -- they made the process simple, smooth, and easy, and the hearing aids I got are the best I've ever had. I'm 64 and now after all these years I feel I'm hearing better than when I was a teenager.

No product is perfect, of course; however  these hearing aids are so much better than the product I bought 8 years ago, it's amazing -- they're really opening up new opportunities for having a better social life.

I bought a top-line pair of hearing aids from the Miracle Ear office in Cupertino, CA. Before choosing this company I did a *lot* of research, and I called several local providers to get an appointment. Miracle Ear was the first and only one I went to, because they convinced me in one session that their hearing aid was the right one for me.

I was helped by Aaron Gabrielson. Aaron started by finding out about my needs, and did a free hearing test right there on the spot as part of the first visit. The results were that I was suffering from significant hearing loss, and these results matched the profile I obtained from my audiologist in the Palo Alto Medical Foundation.

Aaron answered all my questions and was extremely professional, knowledgeable, and also very enjoyable to work with. I feel that he and Rachel really care about my needs and work hard to produce exceptional results for me. Over the follow-up visits (see below) I got to know them better and I really like them -- exceptional professionals and warm people.

The great thing about Miracle Ear is that they do not just sell you hearing aids and forget about you. Instead, they pretty much require you to come in for a series of follow up visits that start once you get your hearing aids, and during these visits Aaron fine-tuned the hearing aids to better match what my hearing loss requires. This is a process whereby your ears and brain get "retrained" to process all the new information that your ears hear. Aaron was always polite, respectful and very helpful.

As with everything, there are some negatives as well. The most significant I'll mention is the price. The hearing aids I bought are the most expensive ones I've ever purchased. Very expensive. But once you consider everything I got, the value is exceptional -- I am now hearing much better than I've ever had, since being a teenager, the time my hearing loss started. The technology is really cutting edge and produces exceptional amplification of what you WANT to hear while suppressing background noises. And the follow-up program and periodic tuning, plus the gradual approach taken, is based on recognizing that people need some adjustment time, and most cannot tolerate the huge jump in what they hear all at once. I believe this approach results in much better results.

I'll close by saying that I've been talking the ears off everyone who will listen (and some people that did not want to listen) about getting hearing aids and recommending the Cupertino office. Two thumbs up!</Text><pictures>None<//pictures>< Resp>

This is a decent older park. It has tad bark vs. a rubbery ground cover. It has two regular swings, two baby swings. The play structure is best suited for kids 4-5 +. My daughter is almost 2 and she can manage the stairs to the main slides, which are steep, but she's brave. Some other features she just too little for. There's a small slide but it has a rough texture so you don't really slide on it. This is my closest park, so we go here when we are short on time. There is lots of open space around the play area with nice picnic tables. There's no bathrooms. It's clean and kept up.< /Text>

<user>110415207590130665768< /user>< Name>
Lynn<//Name>
< rating>
5<//rating>
<Response>None< /Response><pictures>None<//pictures><date>1608028903503< /date>< Text>
This is a small restaurant, but the food packs big flavor. Picked up lunch for takeout, and ordered chicken shawarma and falafel sandwiches, both generously portioned, excellently seasoned, and packaged perfectly. They are made to order, so you can order the fillings spicy, an option not available at most kabob places. The vegetables on the sandwich are chopped so that there is a balanced distribution of flavors, and the pita is soft and fluffy. I ordered extra tzatziki sauce, it is very good, not runny like most places- although the sandwiches are served with it on already.I was only able to eat half the sandwich for lunch, but when I came back to it as leftover, it retained its integrity and flavor wonderfully. We also picked up baklava available at the counter, as well as on their takeout menu- awesome! They are also customer service stars, which is why after delivering for them, I chose to order from them. If you are a fan of Mediterranean food, or like to try new cuisines, check out their menu, and authentic offerings. They are complying with Covid protocol, with takeout and delivery available now.< /Text>

< text>
A hidden gem!!

I stumbled on Teriyaki Express as a complete "why not" moment and I'm happy to report it was a gamble I'm glad I took.

I tried just the safe can chicken teriyaki meal and while the cool time was a bit lengthy the food was more than worth the wait. What I can't express here enough is the freshness of the food itself! The broccoli perfectly crisp, the home made pickled cucumbers(a surprise delight as I hate cucumbers normally) and rice all delicious and with very generous portions! This isn't even counting much better than expected chicken. All and all it was incredible surprise and I've since gone around 4-5 times each time trying something new with different friends so they can also try for themselves (The tonkatsu is by far my favorite at this point).< /text>

First off, I cant say enough positive things about Elite Rooter. Yesterday I noticed a warm spot on my kitchen floor. We immediately figured we had a broken pipe below our floor (pipes are cemented in the slab here).  I called my insurance and they said to call someone who is licensed asap, so I called Roto-Rooter and they said they would have the local rep call me within 25 minutes but they didn't so I called them back after 45 minutes. They discovered that the pipe in the slab has broken and then showed me the water meter  outside was moving.  I called my insurance and they started to fight me and continue to, causing serious frustration.  Their crew put up with me arguing with my homeowners insurance.  Matt decided in the meantime to help me so I can have hot water and we can shower, they would install a valve exiting my water heater so I could shut off the hot water which is the pipe that is broken. Matt then continued to work with the insurance (which is still being an issue) but called another one of their plumbers named Oscar to assist Robert with repairing and fixing the two valves which again turned out to be a project. Recently my shower and toilet were clogged and I called my usual plumber.  It turned from $150 job to a potentially several thousand dollar job.

There was a bigger issue occurring that I was completing unaware.  Apparently the water / sewer pipes under neath the house, which are some 60 years old, were significantly leaking!

In the last few months I got a new roof, house painted and a termite treatment.  A lot of money at one time so when I heard I had to now replace some of my water pipes, I was not very happy.

But there is one thing I learned many years ago.  It is better to face the reality of the situation early and as completely as I can, otherwise it will be more costly down the road and many more headaches!

But my usual plumber never showed me any photos or video of the issue and what I was dealing with but just a general description of the issue and how much is would cost.  Before I decide to lay out that type of money, I want to fully understand what I am dealing with and will this truly resolve the issue or will this issue just keep demanding more money and time?

So I called several other plumbers to get a second opinion.  They all wanted to charge me $100 - $150 to inspect the issue so they could provide an estimate except one ‚Ä¶ Elite Rooter.

Without requesting it, they took a video of what was happening underneath my house and I was shocked at the level of damage and leakage that was occurring.

It was not even close to what my usual plumber told me!

But not Elite Rooter.  Giovanni and David told the whole picture and supported with a video and strongly recommend I replace all the water pipes underneath the house.   Based on the age of pipes, if not now, it would occur to the water & sewer pipes in the kitchen and laundry area.  They would be willing to deduct a proportion of the cost if I didn‚Äôt want them done but he did not recommend it.

They also had several financing plans, one being 18 months with no interest, which lessen the blow.

I always want to dealing with people / companies who are very competent, honest to a fault, thorough and thoughtful in how best to serve a customer‚Äôs challenges.  We have too many challenges as it is and too little time to address them.

This is why it is so valuable to have a painter, like Elite Rooter, to meet the challenges of being a home owner!

Robert</Text>
